CREATE TABLE positions (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(50), description VARCHAR(255), department_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (department_id) REFERENCES departments(id));</t><s>select employees.first_name, employees.last_name, departments.name, positions.description, benefits.type from employees join departments on employees.department = departments.id join positions on employees.department = positions.department_id join benefits on employees.id = benefits.employee_id;</s>
<t>CREATE TABLE departments (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, name VARCHAR(50), location VARCHAR(50));

CREATE TABLE positions (id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY, title VARCHAR(50), description VARCHAR(255), department_id INT, FOREIGN KEY (department_id) REFERENCES departments(id));
